<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><font size="4" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Item 2.02&nbsp;Results of Operations and
Financial Condition.</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On March 27,
2007, the Registrant issued a press release and held a conference call with
analysts to report on the results of operations for the first quarter of fiscal
year 2007, which ended on February 28, 2007.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Furnished with
this Form&nbsp;8-K as Exhibit&nbsp;99.1 is a copy of the press release labeled &#147;McCormick
Reports Record Results for First Quarter of 2007,&#148; which includes an unaudited
Consolidated Income Statement for the three months ended February 28, 2007, an
unaudited Consolidated Balance Sheet of the Registrant as of February 28, 2007,
and an unaudited Consolidated Cash Flow Statement for the three months ended
February 28, 2007.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Item 9.01 Financial
Statements and Exhibits.</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)&#160; Exhibits.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The exhibit to
this report is listed in Item 2.02 above and in the Exhibit Index that follows
the signature line.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">SIGNATURES</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pursuant to the requirements of the Securities
Exchange Act of 1934, the Registrant has duly caused this report to be signed
on its behalf by the undersigned hereunto duly authorized.</font></p>

<div>


<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit
99.1</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><font size="4" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><img width="604" height="93" src="g91101kci001.jpg"></font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;text-indent:144.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">McCORMICK REPORTS RECORD RESULTS FOR
FIRST QUARTER OF 2007</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">SPARKS,
MD, MARCH 27 &#151; McCormick &amp; Company, Incorporated (NYSE:MKC), today reported
record results for the first quarter ended February 28, 2007.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b>Sales increased 7%.&#160; Consumer
business sales rose 9% and industrial business sales rose 5%.</b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b>Cost savings and a more favorable business mix led to gross profit
margin of 40.5%, up 1.3 percentage points from the first quarter of 2006.</b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b>Earnings per share reached 33&#162;.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Robert
J. Lawless, Chairman and CEO, commented, &#147;With our first quarter financial
results, fiscal year 2007 is off to a great start.&#160; The restructuring actions begun in late 2005
are delivering significant cost savings and sustainable margin improvement.&#160; Initiatives to grow our business are driving
sales in a number of our regions around the world.&#160; This added up to an outstanding quarter and
gives us increased confidence that 2007 will be another record year for
McCormick.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Sales
in the first quarter rose 7%, including the impact of foreign currency which
added 3%.&#160; Higher volume from Simply Asia
Foods acquired in mid-2006, new products, ethnic items and convenience items
contributed to this increase, as well as pricing actions.&#160; First quarter sales included the impact of
actions taken to reduce low margin business, which decreased sales 1%.&#160; Gross profit margin rose 1.3 percentage
points to 40.5% as a result of cost savings and a more favorable business mix.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Earnings
per share were 33&#162; compared to 11&#162; in the first quarter of 2006.&#160; Charges related to the Company&#146;s
restructuring program reduced earnings per share 4&#162; in the first quarter of
2007 compared to 17&#162; in the first quarter of 2006.&#160; Excluding the impact of restructuring
charges, earnings per share rose 10&#162;, a 37% increase.&#160; This increase was due to higher sales and
improved gross profit margins, as well as 2&#162; from the quarterly timing of 2007
stock-based compensation expense and 1&#162; from a lower tax rate.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On a
comparable basis which excludes restructuring charges, the Company set a goal
to increase 2007 earnings per share by 8-10%.&#160;
While the first quarter earnings per share increase on a comparable
basis exceeded 8-10%, this was partly due to the timing of certain expenses and
a greater impact from restructuring cost savings in the earlier quarters of
2007.&#160; Financial performance ahead of the
Company&#146;s goal will provide an opportunity to fund additional growth
initiatives.&#160; As a result, including
estimated restructuring charges of 18&#162;, projected 2007 earnings per share
remain $1.67-$1.71.&#160;&#160; However, based on
the outstanding first quarter results, the Company has indicated that it is
likely to achieve earnings per share at the upper end of this range.</font></p>


<br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

  <td width="16" valign="bottom" style="padding:0pt .7pt 0pt 0pt;width:12.0pt;">
  <p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
  </td>
  <td width="52" colspan="2" valign="bottom" style="padding:0pt .7pt 0pt 0pt;width:39.0pt;">
  <p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">60,187</font></b></p>
  </td>
  <td width="16" valign="bottom" style="padding:0pt .7pt 0pt 0pt;width:12.0pt;">
  <p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="52" colspan="2" valign="bottom" style="padding:0pt .7pt 0pt 0pt;width:39.0pt;">
  <p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">46,205</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2" valign="bottom" style="padding:0pt .7pt 0pt 0pt;width:1.7pt;">
  <p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr height="0">
  <td width="427" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="16" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="7" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="45" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="16" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="7" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="45" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="2" style="border:none;"></td>

</div>

<p style="line-height:1.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
the first quarter, sales for McCormick&#146;s consumer business rose 9% and 6% in
local currency.&#160; This increase was driven
by higher volume and pricing actions.&#160;
Higher volume was due to the incremental sales of Simply Asia Foods
acquired in mid-2006, new products and effective marketing programs.&#160; Consumer sales in the Americas rose 10% due
to higher volume from Simply Asia Foods, new products and marketing support, as
well as pricing.&#160; Foreign currency had no
sales impact.&#160; Consumer sales in Europe
increased 6%, but in local currency declined 4%.&#160; This business continues to be affected by
distribution lost to a competitor in The Netherlands and the Company&#146;s decision
in 2006 to exit its business in Finland.&#160;
Also, prior year sales benefited from customer purchases in advance of
the implementation of SAP in this region.&#160;
In the Asia/Pacific region, sales rose 14% and in local currency 9% with
significant gains in China.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
the first quarter, consumer business operating income excluding restructuring
charges rose to $60.2 million from $46.2 million in 2006, an increase of
30%.&#160; This significant increase was due
to higher sales and improved gross profit margin, as well as lower stock-based
compensation expense.&#160; Advertising expense
increased $2.0 million in the first quarter.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Industrial
Business<br>
</font></b>(in thousands)</p>

<p style="line-height:1.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
the first quarter, sales for McCormick&#146;s industrial business increased 5% and
3% in local currency, due to increased volume with strategic customers.&#160; The impact of the Company&#146;s actions to
eliminate lower margin customers and products reduced sales in the first
quarter by 2%.&#160; Industrial sales in the
Americas were down 0.5% from the first quarter of 2006 and down 0.2% in local
currency.&#160; The elimination of lower
margin customers in this part of the industrial business reduced sales 2%.&#160; In Europe, sales rose 19% and 8% in local
currency with continued increases in seasonings for poultry and for snack
products.&#160; In this region, the
elimination of lower margin customers reduced sales 2%.&#160; Sales in the Asia/Pacific region rose 24% and
18% in local currency with significant gains in both China and Australia.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
the first quarter, industrial business operating income excluding restructuring
charges rose to $14.0 million from $11.5 million in 2006, an increase of
22%.&#160; This increase was due to higher
sales and improved gross profit margin, as well as lower stock-based
compensation expense.</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Non-GAAP
Financial Measures</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The pro forma information excluding restructuring
charges in this press release are not measures that are defined in generally
accepted accounting principles (&#147;GAAP&#148;).&#160;
These items are measures that management believes are important to
adjust for in order to have a meaningful comparison to prior and future periods
and to provide a basis for future projections and for estimating our earnings
growth prospects.&#160; These non-GAAP
measures are used by management as a performance measure to judge profitability
of our business absent the restructuring related items.&#160; Management analyzes the Company&#146;s business
performance and trends excluding amounts related to the restructuring.&#160; These measures provide a more consistent view
of performance than the closest GAAP equivalent for management and
investors.&#160; Management compensates for
this by using these measures in combination with the GAAP measures.&#160; The presentation of the non-GAAP measures in
this press release are made alongside the most directly comparable GAAP
measures.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Pro
forma Information</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Company has provided below certain pro forma financial results excluding
amounts related to a restructuring program in 2006 and 2007.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(in thousands except per
share data)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Certain
information contained in this release, including expected trends in net sales
and earnings performance, are &#147;forward-looking statements&#148; within the meaning
of Section 21E of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934.&#160; Forward-looking statements are based on
management&#146;s current views and assumptions and involve risks and uncertainties
that could be materially affected by external factors such as:&#160; actions of competitors, customer
relationships, ability to realize expected cost savings and margin
improvements, market acceptance of new products, actual amount and timing of
special charge items, removal and disposal costs, final negotiations of
third-party contracts, the impact of the stock market conditions on its share repurchase
program, fluctuations in the cost and availability of supply chain resources
and global economic conditions, including interest and currency rate
fluctuations, and inflation rates.&#160; The
Company undertakes no obligation to update or revise publicly, any
forward-looking statements, whether as a result of new information, future
events or otherwise.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About
McCormick</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">McCormick
&amp; Company, Incorporated is the global leader in the manufacture, marketing
and distribution of spices, seasonings and flavors to the entire food industry &#151;
to foodservice and food manufacturers as well as to retail outlets.</font></p>
